***вакантный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вакантный.html>вака́нтный</a> (27856)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">vakant</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">vacant</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вакантный.html>вака́нтный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vakántnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>vacant, unoccupied <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a position or post</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<h4><span id=".D0.A1.D0.B8.D0.BD.D0.BE.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.BC.D1.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Синонимы"><a href = vnd.unilang:синоним.html>Сино́нимы</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:свободный.html>свобо́дный</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:незанятый.html>неза́нятый</a></li>
<li>—</li>

***вал.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вал.html>вал</a> (4597)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">валъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">valŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*valъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вал.html>вал</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">val</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вал.html>ва́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вал.html>валы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вал.html>вало́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>billow, roller</li>
<li>barrage fire</li>
<li>rampart</li>
<li>shaft, axle</li>
<li>gross output
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выполнить.html>вы́полнить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:план.html>план</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вал.html>валу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">výpolnitʹ plan po valu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to implement the plan by bulk output</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***валек.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:валек.html>валёк</a> (7337)</h1><br><hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:валек.html>валёк</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*b  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-вал-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ёк</b>.
</p>
<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/Valenki.jpg/220px-Valenki.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/Valenki.jpg/330px-Valenki.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/Valenki.jpg/440px-Valenki.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3264" data-file-height="2448" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:валенок.html>ва́ленки</a></div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:валенок.html>ва́ленок</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">válenok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:валенок.html>ва́ленка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:валенок.html>ва́ленки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:валенок.html>ва́ленок</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>one of a pair of traditional Russian felt boots, <span class="gender"><abbr title="singular number">sg</abbr></span> valenok, <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> valenki
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white"><a href = vnd.unilang:лев.html>Лев</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:толстый.html>То́лстой</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяин.html>Хозя́ин</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работник.html>рабо́тник</a></i> 1895:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">- <a href = vnd.unilang:дядя.html>дя́дя</a>  Микит, <a href = vnd.unilang:дядюшка.html>дя́дюшка</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дядюшка.html>дя́дюшка</a>!  -  <a href = vnd.unilang:закричать.html>закрича́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сзади.html>сза́ди</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тоненький.html>то́неньким</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голосок.html>голоско́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:торопливый.html>торопли́во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выбежавший.html>вы́бежавший</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сень.html>сене́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двор.html>двор</a> семиле́тний <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчик</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>чёрном</a> полушу́бочке, <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́лых</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:валенок.html>ва́ленках</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:теплый.html>тёплой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шапка.html>ша́пке</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">- Djádja  Mikit, djádjuška, a djádjuška!  -  zakričál szádi jevó tónenʹkim goloskóm toroplívo výbežavšij iz senéj na dvor semilétnij málʹčik v čórnom polušúbočke, nóvyx bélyx <b>válenkax</b> i tjóploj šápke</i></dd><dd>- Uncle Nikita! Uncle! Uncle! - shouted ahint him the brittle voice of a seven-year-old boy hasting, in blackfur jacket, white <b>felt boots</b> and warm hat, from the passage to the court</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>clumsy or stupid person
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тупой.html>тупо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:валенок.html>ва́ленок</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tupój kak <b>válenok</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Dumb as a boot.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***валить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:валить.html>вали́ть</a> (1998)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">volvō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:валить.html>вали́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">valítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повалить.html>повали́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свалить.html>свали́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завалить.html>завали́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to knock down, to kill (e.g. of a disease killing people or animals)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усталость.html>уста́лость</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:просто.html>про́сто</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:валить.html>ва́лит</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>ног</a>).</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ustálostʹ menjá prósto <b>válit</b> (s nog).</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The fatigue is simply knocking me down.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to heap up <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:валить.html>вали́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одну́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:куча.html>ку́чу</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne nádo <b>valítʹ</b> vsjó v odnú kúču.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">No need to lump everything together.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cut, to fell (trees), to make someone fall, to throw down (on the ground)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повалить.html>повали́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">povalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свалить.html>свали́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">svalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to push the blame or responsibility on someone else
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:валить.html>вали́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>друго́го</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>сам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:виноватый.html>винова́т</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne <b>valí</b> na drugóvo, jésli sam vinovát.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Don't blame the other guy, if it's your own fault.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:валить.html>вали́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">valítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повалить.html>повали́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свалить.html>свали́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вальну́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throng <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. of people</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:народ.html>наро́д</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:валить.html>вали́т</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:толпа.html>то́лпами</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фильм.html>фильм</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Naród <b>valít</b> (tólpami) na nóvyj filʹm.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">People are coming in hordes to the new film.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fall heavily <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. of snow</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to belch <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. of smoke</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go away, to scram
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:понять.html>по́нял</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пора.html>пора́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:валить.html>вали́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:страна.html>страны́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On pónjal, što porá <b>valítʹ</b> iz straný.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He understood that it was time to get the heck out of the country.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свалить.html>свали́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">svalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>ва<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:лить.html>ли́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c[(4)].       <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — приставочные <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>ти́па</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:завалить.html>завали́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:повалить.html>повали́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-вал-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>.

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:валить.html>вали́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:повалить.html>повали́ть</a>, вальнуть.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-вал-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>.

***валиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:валиться.html>вали́ться</a> (7045)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:валить.html>вали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">valítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:валиться.html>вали́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">valítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повалиться.html>повали́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fall (down), to drop, to collapse</li>
<li>to overturn, to topple (down)</li>
<li>to come falling down, to roll down</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to die in great numbers</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:валить.html>вали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">valítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ва<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:лить.html>ли́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:повалиться.html>повали́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-вал-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:валявшийся.html>валя́вшийся</a> (2199)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***валять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:валять.html>валя́ть</a> (6545)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:валять.html>валя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">valjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вы́валять</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сваля́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lay or drag on the floor or ground
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:валять.html>валя́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>полу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>valjátʹ</b> pó polu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drag along the floor</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:валять.html>валя́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>гря́зи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>valjátʹ</b> v grjázi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drag in the mire</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вы́валять</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vývaljatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to roll (something) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + prepositional, in flour, bread crumbs, etc., thereby covering the object</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вы́валять</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vývaljatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обваля́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obvaljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to roll (something) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">into some form</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to shape by rolling
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сваля́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">svaljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to knead
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сваля́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">svaljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to felt, to make out of felt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:валять.html>валя́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шляпа.html>шля́пы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>valjátʹ</b> šljápy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make felt hats</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сваля́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">svaljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to do (something) quickly, to carelessly and haphazardly; to churn out (a book), to dash off (a painting), to slap together (a proposal), etc.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">наваля́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">navaljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">only imperative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:валять.html>валя́й</a>(<a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>те</a>)</b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>valjáj(te)</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">go!, go ahead!, go on!, carry on!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ва<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ля́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-вал-</b>; суффикс: <b>-я</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:валяться.html>валя́ться</a> (2199)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:валять.html>валя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">valjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:валяться.html>валя́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">valjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to roll around, to roll from side to side; to wallow</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lie about <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">idly or as a result of being sick; regularly, periodically or for some amount of time</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проваляться.html>проваля́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">provaljátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lie about <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in disorder</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to be strewn carelessly</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:валять.html>валя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">valjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:валяться.html>валя́ться</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-вал-</b>; суффикс: <b>-я</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***вампир.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вампир.html>вампи́р</a> (10528)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">vampire</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Vampir</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">vàmpīr</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ǫpyrь</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упырь.html>упы́рь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">upýrʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***вандализм.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вандализм.html>вандали́зм</a> (31709)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">vandalisme</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вандализм.html>вандали́зм</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vandalízm</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вандализм.html>вандали́зма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вандализм.html>вандали́змы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вандализм.html>вандали́змов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>vandalism</li>
<li>indifference to the arts, lack of taste</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> immoral action</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ванный.html>ва́нный</a> (2952)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ванна.html>ва́нна</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vánna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ванный.html>ва́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vánnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bath, bathroom
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ванный.html>ва́нные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:принадлежность.html>принадле́жности</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vánnyje</b> prinadléžnosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>bathroom</b> accessories</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ванный.html>ва́нный</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-ван(н)-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>-н</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***вар.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вар.html>вар</a> (12722)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">варъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">varŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">boiled liquid</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вар.html>вар</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">var</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вар.html>ва́ра</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>tar, pitch</li>
<li>cobbler's wax</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> boiling water</li></ol>
